 This fridge works on the principle of evaporation and keeps food and food 'cool-cool, cool-cool' without electricity
 pehali najar main dhyaan khinchne vaale isdesifrij ko yahaan board kii ek prashikshan kaaryshaala ke dauraan pesh kiya gaya

 ‚Äô vesta ke mutabik desi frij ko chikani, bhuri va laal mitti se banaaya gaya he or yah lagbhag electronic frij kii tarah kaam karata he
